////////////// NEW HEROES //////////////

"new_hero_changelog" "<img src='file://{images}/heroes/npc_dota_hero_lycan.png' class='ChangelogImage'/><br/><h1>Balthasar</h1>Guardian of the Emerald Flame<br/><br/>A bully in lane and a bully in game, Balthasar is a dangerous and terrifying Hero, capable of chasing down opponents that would normally outrun or outrange their foes. His set of abilities allow him to strike from a distance with <b>Firebolt</b>, create a line of burning ground that grants him extreme movespeed with <b>Doomflame</b>, deal a portion of his attack damage as damage over time with <b>Emerald Fang</b>, and slow and damage his opponents in a large area, while revealing invisible enemies, with <b>Ward of the Emerald Flame</b>.<br/><br/><img src='file://{images}/heroes/npc_dota_hero_sven.png' class='ChangelogImage'/><br/><h1>Siegfried</h1>the Knight of Purgatory<br/><br/>A dangerous foe and valuable ally, the Demonfire Knight commands respect from his enemies in battle, and his abilities feature the duality of action and consequence. With time-bending AoE slows in <b>Eon Shield</b>, <b>Hell Bent</b> granting him a frenzied onslaught of attacks, magic immunity upon spell cast with <b>Epoch's Protection</b> and the ability to globally assist an ally for a short time with the use of <b>Heaven Sent</b>, Siegfried is extremely dangerous and difficult to deal with when played correctly, but his insistence on being in the fray makes him the prime target for burst damage and disables."

////////////// HERO CHANGES //////////////

"hero_changelog" "<i>Patch 2.14a:</i><br/><img src='file://{images}/heroes/npc_dota_hero_lycan.png' class='ChangelogImage'/><br/><h1>Balthasar</h1><br/>Level 20 Talent changed from +500 Doomflame Range to Doomflame Free Pathing.<br/>Level 25 Talent +600 Ward of the Emerald Flame Radius reduced to +350.<br/>Base movespeed reduced to 310 (was 315).<br/>Base Health regen reduced to 0.5 (was 1.0).<br/>Base Mana regen reduced to 0.5 (was 1.0).<br/>Base damage reduced to 48 - 51 (was 51 - 52).<br/>Base Armor increased by 1.<br/>Night vision reduced to 800 (was 1000).<br/><img src='file://{images}/heroes/npc_dota_hero_riki.png' class='ChangelogImage'/><br/><h1>Lupin</h1><br/>Beneath the Mask slow increased to 8/14/20/26% (was 8/12/16/20%).<br/>Beneath the Mask duration reduced to 2.5/3.0/3.5/4.0s (was 2/3/4/5s).<br/>Beneath the Mask now renders Lupin invisible, with no fade time, for the duration. Attacking, using items, or casting Spells does not reveal Lupin.<br/>Finisher cooldown reduced to 3s (was 9/8/7/6s).<br/>Finisher damage reduced to 30/60/90/120 (was 40/80/120/160).<br/>Finisher Mana cost reduced to 30/40/50/60 (was 75).<br/>Finisher slow duration reduced to 0.50s (was 0.75s).<br/><br/><i>Patch 2.14:</i><img src='file://{images}/heroes/npc_dota_hero_ursa.png' class='ChangelogImage'/><br/><h1>Fury</h1>Roar duration reduced to 4s (was 5.25s).<br/>Berserk duration increased to 6s (was 4.5/5.0/5.5s).<br/>Berserk cooldown increased to 80/60/40s (was 60/50/40s).<br/>Berserk no longer grants bonus Rend and Bloodsport stacks.<br/>Berserk now prevents Fury's Health from dropping below 1 while it's active.<br/>Rend and Bloodsport no longer function on illusions.<br/>Rend and Bloodsport are now disabled by Break.<br/>Talent: Level 25 +4s Berserk Duration (was +3s Berserk Duration).<br/><br/><img src='file://{images}/heroes/npc_dota_hero_bounty_hunter.png' class='ChangelogImage'/><br/><h1>Shade</h1>Dark Hunger now grants Health and Mana based on the damage Shade deals (from any source). 10/15/20/25% of damage is converted to Health and Mana restored. Only 1/4th effective against creeps.<br/>Stalk now only deals Pure damage.<br/>Stalk damage increased to 50/100/150/200.<br/>Stalk cooldown reduced to 24/18/12/6s.<br/>Isolation no longer Silences.<br/>Isolation now applies a 25% slow.<br/>Isolation now reduces damage output by 60% (was 50%).<br/><br/><img src='file://{images}/heroes/npc_dota_hero_spectre.png' class='ChangelogImage'/><br/><h1>Phantasm</h1>Shadowstep cooldown increased to 60s (was 50/40/30/20s).<br/>Shadowstep delay time rescaled to 4.00/3.25/2.50/1.75s (was 3.00s).<br/>Shadowstep bonus movespeed increased to 30% (was 25%).<br/>Shadowstep now grants Phased movement and free pathing for the duration.<br/>Shadowstep now applies a Basic Dispel upon teleportation.	<br/>Nightmare now also prevents the target's allies from helping them with targeted Spells and Items.<br/><br/><img src='file://{images}/heroes/npc_dota_hero_axe.png' class='ChangelogImage'/><br/><h1>War</h1>Bloodlust duration reduced to 10 ticks (was 14 ticks).<br/>Bloodlust damage reduced to 15/25/35/45 (was 12/24/36/48).<br/>Bloodlust now slows by 15%.<br/>Bloodlust now ticks once every 0.75s (instead of once every 1.00s).<br/>Bloodlust is now removed if the affected unit kills a non-Illusion Hero, and is removed from all Heroes if War dies.<br/>Bloodlust does not tick down while attacking under the effects of War's Ultimate.<br/>Earthbreaker damage reduced to 75/125/175/225 (was 100/150/200/250).<br/>Earthbreaker stun changed to 1.50s (was 1.00/1.35/1.70/2.05s).<br/>Earthbreaker mana cost is now 75 (was 55/65/75/85).<br/>Earthbreaker radius reduced to 300 (was 325).<br/>Level 15 Talent changed to +100 Earthbreaker Radius (was +25 Berserker Aura AS/MS)<br/>Level 20 Talent reduced to +25 Bloodlust DPS (was +35)<br/>Level 25 Talent changed to -4s Earthbreaker Cooldown (was +200 Earthbreaker Radius)"

The child could speak to Spirits, but should they utter a word in return, they would be wrenched of their immortality, left weak and vulnerable. The Marqas, arbiters of order, deemed her child cursed, and banished her to the Nothing. As the darkness twisted around her, pulling every cell from her body for an agonising eternity, the true nature of her curse was discovered. The spirits of the old land began to die, one by one, their souls fading as the child's did. In a panicked realisation of their mistakes, the Marqas pulled her from her prison and tasked her with wandering the planes and restoring the dead or mortal Spirits, bestowing upon her incredible powers of regeneration and fighting prowess."

One of which was that of the Great One, an elder of elders, their whim bending reality around them, their heart a roaring flame. It is said that their son grew jealous of such power, and wished to gain it for himself. Whenever asked, the Great One only spake: 'in due time.' As the son's jealousy grew, he devised a plan. Using the essence of envy, he forged a weapon: a blade of emerald fury, with the power to extract the abilities of the Great One. One night, he snuck into the Great One's keep, and went to strike him down with his blade. However, the Great One was prepared; he had seen his son forging this monstrosity. As the son landed the final blow, the Great One uttered a curse, sealing his soul into the sword itself. The son could not extract the powers, no matter how hard he tried. Defeated by his failures, he took his own life using that same blade. Yet death did not come easily to him; instead, the Emerald Blade and the Flame of the Great One combined, creating a jade flame. The son's form dissipated, and he was transformed into a creature of the night, a protector of the fire: The Wolf of the Emerald Flame."

		"npc_dota_hero_arc_warden_bio" "A being from a forgotten Plane, the creature known only as 'Baal' foresaw that which his kind did not; the End. In his dreams he saw fire descending upon his people, destroying all that he knew. His fears came to a head, and with the help of others, he put a plan in motion; before the cataclysmic event, he would drag his world into the next Plane, and deal with the consequences afterwards. The event began as his dream foretold: a being of light and fire had formed, infantile and oblivious, its light singeing the edges of his home. With a cry, he and his comrades used all of their might to push their home through the warping walls of the Plane. All seemed well, until the gap widened, and an unfathomable force tore at the Plane. His home began to crumble as it fell through, and he watched with horror as the being of fire was torn from its celestial cradle, its form washing over and searing all that he knew to ash. As he fell into this new plane, his anger and guilt consumed him, his physical form a self imposed prison for his transgressions against his own kind."

Wielding a shield that could twist time itself, and a sword that could bend space to his will, his influence spanned centuries upon centuries, helping the weak and purging evil from the lands. When another member, the Mouthpiece of Epoch, began plotting against the people in His name, Siegfried tried all he could to stop him, and to prove Epoch's continued love for humanity, despite the Mouthpiece's mad ramblings of power and destruction. As each of his fellow Counsel members turned against him, Siegfried had but one option remaining: travel to the deepest pits of the Below, obtain the Demon's Fire, absorbing it into his sword, and use its power to cut through Epoch's protection, ridding the world of the treacherous Mouthpiece. Upon his return, he went to strike the Mouthpiece to find he had been tricked. His blade, possessed by the Fire's malicious intent, cut down every member of the Counsel as he weeped, leaving him the sole survivor. He now travels, cursed sword in one hand, and the time-bending Eon Shield in the other, seeking to atone to Epoch for his sins..."

A veteran assassin, and a slayer of countless mages, he tore across Lochraith at the drop of a coin, seemingly unstoppable. Not all lives were his, however; a young Arca had seen him coming days in advance, and set a devious trap. Caught in a powerful binding spell, he prepared to take his last breath, but the Arca hesitated. For all the trouble he had caused, all those he had killed in the name of avarice, he deserved worse than death. His punishment would forever be wandering a dark void, unable to escape, with no need for material goods, with no quarries to find. She hastily weaved a dark, terrible curse, full of isolation and solitude. But curses are fickle creatures, born of terrible, turbulent emotions. She realised her mistake all but a second too late. Using the very threads she had weaved prior, the Nightwalker tore her from the plane, imprisoning her in a desolate realm, using his undying connection with her to weave dark magic of his own."
